(text-style:"bold","double-underline")[ How did FDR's New Deal benefit $group? ] <div class="container"> <div class="row"> <div class="col-6"> (if:$group is "immigrants")[ The new deal benefited immigrants by creating jobs for them on government funded projects. This brought many out of poverty and while the wages were low, they still made some money. Relief from the Great Depression helped them the most. ] (if:$group is "bankers")[ Reform helped bankers in the sense that now the government guaranteed deposits so people began to put trust in banks again. This helped new banks form and created jobs for bankers. This allowed bankers to get reemployed and start making decent money again. ] (if:$group is "business owners")[ Business owners were most helped by the recovery aspect of the New Deal. The government set regulations for prices, wages, and hours to help level the playing field for businesses and end the downward direction that prices were going in. ] </div> <div class="col-6"> <img alt="Image related to FDR's New Deal"/> </div> </div> </div>(text-style:"bold","double-underline")[ How did the start of WW2 benefit $group? ] (if:$group is "immigrants")[ The start of World War 2 created many jobs for immigrants as factory workers, and soldiers. As new weapon manufacturing companies appeared immigrants were newly given jobs and unemployment dropped. ] (if:$group is "bankers")[ World War 2 created jobs for bankers as middle people in the selling and holding of bonds from the government. With unemployment also falling, banks got large deposits from many people who were now employed and saving money. ] (if:$group is "business owners")[ Business owners could scale production and sale as war creates a large demand for many products, especially food and weapons. This gave businesses guaranteed government buyers for many products and as more people became employed with the start of WW2, more people began spending money again helping the economy and business owners thrive. ](text-style:"bold","double-underline")[How did the stock market crash affect $group?] <div class="container"> <div class="row"> <div class="col-6"> (if:$group is "immigrants")[ People who had immigrated to the US during the 1920s had probably taken part in the prosperity and bought stocks on margin believing the upward motion of the stock prices would never end. The stock market crash was caused by many who had seen the drop and other Americans and then quickly sold their stocks for much lower than what they had bought it for accumulating debt. Many had savings accounts, but the bank, which had also invested in the stock market, no longer had their money, so many lost everything. ] (if:$group is "bankers")[ The stock market crash greatly affected bankers as their entire job usually is to take the money people put into banks and invest it on the stock market. The stock market crash made the bankers lose people's money totaling millions as they had invested not only for themselves but for many. Many either were fired or forced to close the bank as the bank couldn't handle the mass withdrawals. Bankers lost all of the money they had invested on the stock market if they had sold and lost people's savings as well, harming not only themselves but others. This also created a loss of trust in banks which made it difficult for banks to come back later. ] (if:$group is "business owners")[ The stock market crash did not greatly affect business owners directly unless they had invested in the stock market. Many businesses, however, had probably made savings accounts in banks to save money to pay workers' wages, though with the crash they lost that saved money in banks as the banks lost the money. If a business was a public company, their company would also become undervalued. Out of the three groups, business owners were not as affected as immigrants and far from as affected as bankers. ] </div> <div class="col-6"> <img </div> </div> </div>(text-style:"bold","double-underline")[How was life like for $group in the 1920s?] <div class="container"> <div class="row"> <div class="col-6"> (if:$group is "immigrants")[ During the Roaring 20s, many people immigrated to the US following World War 1. The Roaring 20s being a time of prosperity attracted many immigrants who found work and shared in the nation's prosperity. Assuming the immigrants were working class, they took part in urbanization and relatively high wages of the time. Like many, they probably invested in the stock market and drove new Ford Model Ts as they had become affordable with the production line. ] (if:$group is "bankers")[ Bankers and banks grew rapidly with the Roaring 20s as many people had higher salaries and wanted to save their money for a later date. Bankers invested the money stored in the bank on the stock market and made large profits. They lived lavish and wealthy lifestyles living in desirable areas. ] (if:$group is "business owners")[ Business owners made large profits as people having higher salaries spent more on luxury items that new businesses offered. This brought more income to business owners which reinvested the money into their own business or onto the stock market. ] </div> <div class="col-6"> <img </div> </div> </div><h1>The Great Depression</h1> <p class="subtitle">By Jacob Spar</p> The Great Depression affected many different groups of society, and many of them had to come up with different ways to survive the Great Depression. The causes of the Great Depression affected every group differently, the stock market collapse harmed most but some like farmers who had not invested in the stock market were not affected by that specific cause but greatly affected by another cause such as oversupply. Each group was affected differently. Explore how the following groups dealt with the Great Depression: (link: "Bankers")[ (set: $group to "bankers") (goto: "Questions") ] (link: "Immigrants")[ (set: $group to "immigrants") (goto: "Questions") ] (link: "Business Owners")[ (set: $group to "business owners") (goto: "Questions") ]Click on a question to view the answer for (upperfirst:$group). (set: $questions to (a: "How was life like for "+$group+" in the 1920s?", "How did the stock market crash affect "+$group+"?", "What cause of the Great Depression most affected "+$group+"?", "What was life like for "+$group+" during the Great Depression?", "How did FDR's New Deal benefit "+$group+"?", "How did the start of WW2 benefit "+$group+"?", "What lasting impression did the Great Depression have on "+$group+"?" )) (for: each _q, ...$questions)[ * (link: _q)[ (goto: (str-replaced: " "+$group, "", _q)) ] ](text-style:"bold","double-underline")[ What cause of the Great Depression most affected $group? ] (if:$group is "immigrants")[ Immigrants were most affected by unemployment as over 25% of Americans in the US were unemployed during the worst parts of the Great Depression. Immigrants were less likely to get a job than natural-born Americans as business owners could often discriminate against them. ] (if:$group is "bankers")[ Bankers were most affected by the stock market crash as lots of bankers had invested people's money on the stock market so when it crashed they were unable to pay many people their money back. They had also loaned money to other people who bought stocks on margin who were then unable to pay the bankers back making the bankers lose even more money. The stock market crash and this loss of money caused many bankers to lose their jobs as the bank owners had to close the bank. ] (if:$group is "business owners")[ Business owners were harmed by the oversupply of products and goods causing them to either sell at a minimal profit margin or a loss. Many could have problems selling their products at all. The oversupply of goods caused many businesses to close, causing higher unemployment. ](text-style:"bold","double-underline")[ What lasting impression did the Great Depression have on $group? ] (if:$group is "immigrants")[ The Great Depression created a lot of anti-immigrant sentiment that carries on today. Mass deportations during the Great Depression shattered immigrants' trust in the government and many depend on each other for mutual aid. ] (if:$group is "bankers")[ Bankers were left with many new government regulations that limit interest rates and make them more secure but also prevent very quick growth. Bankers now had much more secure and safe positions but they were also now highly government regulated. In a way their lives are better now as they have secure jobs but also now their profits are much more limited. ] (if:$group is "business owners")[ The Great Depression left more regulations on business owners than banks. Minimum wages, maximum hours, and more regulations caused both businesses to hate and love the government as it regulated them but also protected them. ](text-style:"bold","double-underline")[ What was life like for $group during the Great Depression? ] <div class="container"> <div class="row"> <div class="col-6"> (if:$group is "immigrants")[ During the Great Depression immigrants had trouble finding jobs as many business owners discriminated and valued American workers over immigrants. Throughout the Great Depression many immigrants were deported for various reasons, some even legal immigrants were deported as many people developed a hate towards immigrants believing they were stealing American jobs. ] (if:$group is "bankers")[ During the Great Depression trust in banks was really low as the stock market crash had made banks lose people's money shattering their trust. Until the government began insuring deposits people were reluctant to start depositing money in banks again making it difficult for bankers to find work. ] (if:$group is "business owners")[ During the Great Depression business owners faced fierce competition as an oversupply of goods caused prices to drop fatally for many businesses.
